    name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    founded_date DATE,
    headquarters VARCHAR(255)
);

CREATE TABLE review (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    game_id INT,
    player_id INT,
    rating DECIMAL(2, 1),
    review_text TEXT,
    FOREIGN KEY (game_id) REFERENCES game(id),
    FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES player(id)
);

CREATE TABLE player (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE,
    registration_date DATE
);</t><stat>INSERT INTO player (id, username, email, registration_date) VALUES (1, 'player1', 'player1@example.com', '2022-01-15');</stat><divider><t>CREATE TABLE game (

CREATE TABLE players (player_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_name VARCHAR(255), player_level INT, player_score INT);</t><stat>INSERT INTO achievements (achievement_id, achievement_name, player_id, achievement_date) VALUES (1, 'Scored 100 goals', 1, '2022-01-15');</stat><divider><t>CREATE TABLE inventory (item_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_id INT, item_name VARCHAR(255), item_quantity INT, item_type VARCHAR(255), FOREIGN KEY (player_id) REFERENCES players(player_id));
